***изводить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:изводить.html>изводи́ть</a> (16406)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">из-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">iz-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:водить.html>води́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vodítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:изводить.html>изводи́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">izvodítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:известить.html>извести́</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to use up, to spend</li>
<li>to exterminate</li>
<li>to exhaust
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:изводить.html>изводи́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:себя.html>себя́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:работа.html>рабо́той</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>izvodítʹ</b> sebjá rabótoj</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to overwork oneself</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to torment
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:изводить.html>изводи́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:насмешка.html>насме́шками</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>izvodítʹ</b> nasméškami</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to bait</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to vex, to exasperate</li></ol>

***изволить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:изволить.html>изво́лить</a> (5423)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">из-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">iz-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:воля.html>во́ля</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vólja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ить</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-itʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:изволить.html>изво́лить</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">izvólitʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">dated<span class="ib-comma">,</span> ironic</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to desire, to wish
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:изволить.html>изво́льте</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>izvólʹte</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">please, if you wish</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:изволить.html>изво́лите</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:чай.html>ча́ю</a>?</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>izvólite</b> čáju?</i> ― <span class="e-translation">would you like some tea?</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:куда.html>куда́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:изволить.html>изво́лите</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:ехать.html>е́хать</a>?</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">kudá <b>izvólite</b> jéxatʹ?</i> ― <span class="e-translation">where do you wish to go?</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:что.html>чего́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:изволить.html>изво́лите</a></b>?</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">čevó <b>izvólite</b>?</i> ― <span class="e-translation">1) <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">dated</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> <i>(a question of a seller, servant etc.)</i> how may I serve you? 2) <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">pejorative</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> at-your-service attitude</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">dated</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to kindly, to please be good enough <i>(+ to)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:изволить.html>изво́льте</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:выйти.html>вы́йти</a>!</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>izvólʹte</b> výjti!</i> ― <span class="e-translation">leave the room if you please!</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:изволить.html>изво́льте</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:молчать.html>молча́ть</a>!</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>izvólʹte</b> molčátʹ!</i> ― <span class="e-translation">kindly be quiet!</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вы.html>вы</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:потерять.html>потеря́ли</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ключ.html>ключ</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:теперь.html>тепе́рь</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:изволить.html>изво́льте</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>его́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:найти.html>найти́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">vy poterjáli ključ, tepérʹ <b>izvólʹte</b> jevó najtí</i> ― <span class="e-translation">you have lost the key, now be good enough to find it</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">dated</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to if you wish, to all right, to with pleasure
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:изволить.html>изво́ль</a></b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>я</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:остаться.html>оста́нусь</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>izvólʹ</b>, ja ostánusʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation">all right, I will stay</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***изворачиваться.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:изворачиваться.html>извора́чиваться</a> (23151)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">из-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">iz-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:воротить.html>вороти́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vorotítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ивать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ivatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:изворачиваться.html>извора́чиваться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">izvoráčivatʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:извернуться.html>изверну́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to turn sharply</li>
<li>to twist deftly <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">to accomplish or avoid something</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to find a way out of a predicament, to be resourceful</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to try to get rid of something unpleasant</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively<span class="ib-comma">,</span> colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to use cunning or trickery, to contrive</li></ol>

***извратить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:извратить.html>изврати́ть</a> (17048)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">из-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">iz-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-врати́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-vratítʹ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to turn</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, which is also found in <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:возвратить.html>возврати́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vozvratítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> and <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отвратить.html>отврати́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">otvratítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, and is ultimately derived from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*vortiti</i> (whence <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:воротить.html>вороти́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vorotítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>).
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:извратить.html>изврати́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">izvratítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">извраща́ть</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to pervert</li>
<li>to distort, to give false account</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:изгнавший.html>изгна́вший</a> (9609)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:изгнавший.html>изгна́вший</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">izgnávšij</span>)

***изгой.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:изгой.html>изго́й</a> (19572)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv"><a href = vnd.unilang:изгой.html>изго́и</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">izgoi</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Asynchronically analyzable as <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">из-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">iz-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">го́ить</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">góitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, the latter being a causative form of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:жить.html>жить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">žitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:изгой.html>изго́й</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">izgój</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:изгой.html>изго́я</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:изгой.html>изго́и</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:изгой.html>изго́ев</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>outcast, outlaw, castaway, derelict</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">изго́йствовать</span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">izgójstvovatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

***изготавливавшийся.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:изготавливаться.html>изгота́вливавшийся</a> (26312)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
